<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-2fef28c6103d807498bbd1c20d152a14" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--20);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--20);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30)">Stylish Cruising</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center" style="padding-top:0;padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:0;padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);font-size:20px">Hi, I&#8217;m Pam! Welcome to Stylish Cruising, which focuses on all aspects of cruise travel from planning to packing and beyond. Whether you&#8217;re an avid premium cruiser like us or a new cruiser on a budget, you&#8217;re sure to find something for you. </p>

<h6 class="kt-adv-heading909_ba201b-e0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading909_ba201b-e0"></h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading909_7747ac-6f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading909_7747ac-6f">Follow My Cruise Blog For Tips And Inspiration!​</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading909_bdeb79-5d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading909_bdeb79-5d">In 2024, we returned to the Caribbean, exploring new islands. Plus, we made our first transatlantic cruise and toured Iceland, France, and the Netherlands, and then spent a few days exploring London. Norwegian Fjords were next, as well as Spain and Portugal, and then the ABC Islands in the fall, where we toured Bonaire for the first time. What fun we had!</p>



<p>In 2025, we are scheduled so far for another Caribbean cruise, a transatlantic that stops in Bermuda, Portugal, and Spain, a transpacific from Hawaii to Vancouver, an extensive tour of the British Isles, Canada and New England, Norway, and then back to the Greek Isles with stops in Turkey.</p>



<p>Come along and explore the world with us!</p>

				let timeout = 30000000; // 30 seconds
				let start = Date.now();
				return new Promise(wait_for_complianz);

				function wait_for_complianz(resolve, reject) {
					if (window.cmplz_get_cookie) // if complianz is loaded, resolve the promise
						resolve(window.cmplz_get_cookie);
					else if (timeout && (Date.now() - start) >= timeout)
						reject(new Error("timeout"));
					else
						setTimeout(wait_for_complianz.bind(this, resolve, reject), 30);
				}
			}
